<script>
(function() {
    // Fonction pour récupérer les paramètres d'URL
    function getParameterByName(name) {
        var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)', 'i');
        var results = regex.exec(window.location.href);
        return results ? decodeURIComponent(results[1]) : null;
    }

    // Fonction pour créer un cookie
    function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        if (!getCookie(name)) { // Créer seulement si le cookie n'existe pas déjà
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; expires=' + date.toUTCString() + '; path=/';
        }
    }

    // Fonction pour lire un cookie
    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = '; ' + document.cookie;
        var parts = value.split('; ' + name + '=');
        return parts.length === 2 ? parts.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
    }

    // Initialisation de la source de trafic
    var trafficSource = 'direct';

    // Vérifie les paramètres UTM ou autres identifiants dans l'URL
    if (getParameterByName('gclid')) {
        trafficSource = 'google / cpc';
    } else if (getParameterByName('fbclid')) {
        trafficSource = 'facebook / cpc';
    } else if (getParameterByName('ttclid')) {
        trafficSource = 'tiktok / cpc';
    } else if (getParameterByName('utm_source')) {
        var utmSource = getParameterByName('utm_source');
        var utmMedium = getParameterByName('utm_medium') || 'none';
        trafficSource = utmSource + ' / ' + utmMedium;
    } else if (document.referrer) {
        var referrer = document.referrer;
        var referrerDomain = referrer.split('/')[2] || '';
        if (referrerDomain.indexOf('google') > -1) {
            trafficSource = 'google / organic';
        } else if (referrerDomain.indexOf('bing') > -1) {
            trafficSource = 'bing / organic';
        } else {
            trafficSource = referrerDomain + ' / referral';
        }
    }

    // Créer un cookie nommé "initialTrafficSource" avec la source de trafic pour 365 jours
    setCookie('initialTrafficSource', trafficSource, 365);
})();

    if( input_gclid !== null) {
		console.log(input_gclid.id);
		console.log(input_gclid.value);
		
        // Retrieve values
        let gclid = getUrlParameter('gclid') || getCookie('_gcl_aw');
        let initialTrafficSource = getCookie('initialTrafficSource');
        let client_id = getCookie('_ga')?.split('.')?.slice(-2).join('.');

        // Inject values into Gravity Forms
        input_gclid.value     = gclid || '';
        input_initial.value   = initialTrafficSource || '';
        input_client_id.value = client_id || '';
	}
});

function getCookie(name) {
    let match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
    return match ? match[2] : null;
}

function getUrlParameter(name) {
    let params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    return params.get(name);
}

				function dibTogglePlayableTags( divibar_id, wait ) {
				
					var $ = jQuery;
					
					if ( !divibar_id  ) {
						
						divibar_id = "";
					}
					
					if ( !wait  ) {
						
						wait = 1;
					}

					setTimeout(function() {
						
						$( divibar_id + ".divibars").find("iframe").each(function() { 
						
							var iframeParent = $(this).parent();
							var iframe = $(this).prop("outerHTML");
							var src = iframe.match(/src=[\'"]?((?:(?!\/>|>|"|\'|\s).)+)"/)[0];
							
							src = src.replace("src", "data-src");
							iframe = iframe.replace(/src=".*?"/i, "src=\"about:blank\" data-src=\"\"" );
							
							if ( src != "data-src=\"about:blank\"" ) {
								iframe = iframe.replace("data-src=\"\"", src );
							}
							
							$( iframe ).insertAfter( $(this) );
							
							$(this).remove();
						});
						
					}, wait);
					
					$( divibar_id + ".divibars").find("video").each(function() {
						$(this).get(0).pause();
					});
					
					$( divibar_id + ".divibars").find("audio").each(function() {
						
						this.pause();
						this.currentTime = 0;
					});
				}

	<li class="et_pb_menu_page_id-41 menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-has-children menu-item-41"><a href="/newsroom/">Newsroom</a>

		<div class="container">
		<div id="content-area" class="clearfix">
			<div id="left-area">
											<article id="post-2745" class="et_pb_post post-2745 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-bazarloader category-malware category-malware-research tag-bazarloader tag-malware tag-malware-research">
											<div class="et_post_meta_wrapper">
							<h1 class="entry-title">BazarLoader Mocks Researchers in December 2020 Malspam Campaign</h1>

						<p class="post-meta"> by <span class="author vcard"><a href="https://gosecure.ai/blog/author/lilly-chalupowski/" title="Posts by Lilly Chalupowski" rel="author">Lilly Chalupowski</a></span> | <span class="published">Feb 1, 2021</span></p>
												</div> <!-- .et_post_meta_wrapper -->
				
					<div class="entry-content">
					<div class="et-l et-l--post">
			<div class="et_builder_inner_content et_pb_gutters3">
		<div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_0 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_0">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_0  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_0  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Preface</h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_1  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Our Inbox Detection and Response (<strong>IDR</strong>) team has observed a new BazarLoader campaign targeting the information technology, aeronautic and financial industries. The <strong>IDR</strong> team has successfully blocked over 550 thousand BazarLoader malspam emails throughout this campaign alone.</p>
<p>GoSecure researchers received a sample from the <strong>IDR</strong> team which was suspected of being BazarLoader, named Report <em>Preview15-10.exe</em>, on <em>2020-10-06</em>. Shortly after, GoSecure researchers received yet another BazarLoader sample on <em>2020-10-08</em> named <em>Document2-85.exe</em>, which exhibited similar behavior.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_1 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_1">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_1  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_2  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Analysis</h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_3  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The initial infection vector, which has been observed by our Inbox Detection and Response Team (<strong>IDR</strong>), is via malspam containing fake employment termination notices and anonymous surveys. The threat actor(s) primarily use Google Drive and Google Docs to distribute their malicious payloads. The employment termination malspam was observed on October 6, 2020 and the anonymous survey malspam was observed on October 8, 2020. This can be seen in <em>Figure 1</em> and <em>Figure 2</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_0">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/Vera-XSS-and-Improper-Access-Control_Image-1.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img width="1203" height="204" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-email_1.png" alt="BazarLoader-email_1" title="BazarLoader-email_1" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_4  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 1: BazarLoader Employment Termination Malspam</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_1">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-email_2.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="862" height="404" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-email_2.png" alt="BazarLoader-email_2" title="BazarLoader-email_2" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="862" height="404" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20862%20404%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-email_2.png" alt="BazarLoader-email_2" title="BazarLoader-email_2" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_5  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 2: BazarLoader Fake Anonymous Survey</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_6  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>We will firstly analyze the employment termination malspam.</p>
<p>Once the user clicks the link, they will be redirected to<br /> <span style="color: #da291c;">hxxps://docs[.]google[.]com/document/d/e/2PACX-1vR_9tGGWDcS1ZyIuiGpMQg2Sv9nRWempyUKuQ1iyJp_HHt1C87OPirnO7EImnOW6ILbrmHXUpl_OIxQ/pub</span> to download an executable.</p>
<p>The executable <em>Review_Report15-10.exe</em> (<span style="color: #da291c;">3c27fca6d9cf1379eee93e6fea339e61</span>) will appear as a<br /> PDF document to users who do not have extensions enabled in Windows, as seen in <em>Figure 3</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_2">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_icon.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="96" height="115" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_icon.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_icon" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_icon" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="96" height="115" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%2096%20115%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_icon.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_icon" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_icon" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_7  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 3: Stage 1 PDF Icon Lure</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_8  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>To help obfuscate its purpose, BazarLoader appears to be bound or obfuscated with legitimate resources from <em>YUVPlayer (A Lightweight YUV player which supports various YUV formats)</em>. An example of this can be seen in <em>Figure 4</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_3">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="454" height="254" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog.png" alt="BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog" title="BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="454" height="254" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20454%20254%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog.png" alt="BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog" title="BazarLoader-yuvplayer_dialog" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_9  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 4: YUVPlayer Dialog Embedded Resource</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_10  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner">Once executed, the legitimate application or dialogs will not be shown to the user. Instead, it will call <code class="language-markup">advapi32.CryptHashData</code> using the string <code class="language-markup">s_)q03vcOm95^+Rj3dG_Jx@k0GGwYOIddH_14025b520</code> as the data to create a hash using the <code class="language-markup">PROV_RSA_FULL</code> Windows cryptographic provider. Once the hash is created, it will create a key using <code class="language-markup">advapi32.CryptDeriveKey</code>. <span>It will then obtain a handle to the current process for the purpose of allocating memory with</span> <code class="language-markup">PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE</code> permissions. The next function is responsible for copying the shellcode from the <code class="language-markup">.data</code> section to the newly allocated memory location. Once the encrypted shellcode has been copied to executable memory, it will then use <code class="language-markup">advapi32.CryptEncrypt</code> to decrypt the shellcode. Once the shellcode has been successfully decrypted, it will execute the shellcode.</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_4">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="698" height="481" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine.png" alt="BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine" title="BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="698" height="481" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20698%20481%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine.png" alt="BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine" title="BazarLoader-shellcode_decryption_routine" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_11  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 5: BazarLoader Shellcode Decryption Routine</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_5">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="1452" height="823" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="1452" height="823" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%201452%20823%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_execute_shellcode" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_12  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 6: Executing Stage 1 Decrypted Shellcode</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_13  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner">The shellcode will obtain a handle to <code class="language-markup">kernel32.LoadLibraryA</code>, <code class="language-markup">kernel32.GetProcAddress</code>, <code class="language-markup">kernel32.VirtualAlloc</code>, <code class="language-markup">kernel32.VirtualProtect</code> and <code class="language-markup">ntdll.ZwFlushInstructionCache</code>, by enumerating the Process Environment Block (PEB) using the instruction <code class="language-markup">mov rax,qword ptr gs: [60]</code>.  This is common with shellcode as it will need to resolve these APIs dynamically to interact with the Windows operating system.</p>
<p>Once completed, it will then call <code class="language-markup">kernel32.VirtualALloc</code> to prepare injecting a PE executable for the next stage. To build the PE header, it will use the routine shown in <em>Figure 7</em>.</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_6">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="650" height="251" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="650" height="251" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20650%20251%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_inject_pe_header" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_14  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><em>Figure 7: Prepare Stage 2 PE</em></p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_15  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once PE header has been partially copied (excluding MZ magic value), it will start to copy the <code class="language-markup">.text</code> section using the routine shown in <em>Figure 8</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_7">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="722" height="574" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="722" height="574" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20722%20574%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_text_section" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_16  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 8: Copy .text Section</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_17  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once the <code class="language-markup">.text</code> section is copied, it will start resolving many different Windows APIs using <code class="language-markup">kernel32.GetProcAddress</code>.</p>
<p>When the additional APIs have been resolved, it will then make the <code class="language-markup">.text</code> section it copied earlier executable using <code class="language-markup">kernel32.VirtualProtect</code>, as seen in <em>Figure 9</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_8">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="440" height="473" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable" title="BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="440" height="473" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20440%20473%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable" title="BazarLoader-stage_text_section_executable" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_18  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 9: Make .text Section Executable</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_19  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p><strong>NOTE:</strong> <em>On different debugging sessions the virtual addressing changed during analysis. </em></p>
<p>Interestingly, the Portable Executable (PE) BazarLoader is copied into memory (without the MZ<br />
header) and will start execution at the end of the <code class="language-markup">.text</code> section using a direct <code class="language-markup">call</code>. This can make unpacking the next stage confusing for reverse engineers as this is not where code in a PE file is supposed to begin. This code at the end of the <code class="language-markup">.text</code> section is solely responsible for making a call to the real Original Entrypoint (OEP) of the PE. It is important to note that this is simply used as shellcode and not as a PE in memory. The other benefit of this technique is no calls to thread related APIs are required, making it more challenging for Endpoint Detection and Response (EDR) solutions to detect. This can be seen in <em>Figure 10</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_9">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="1163" height="226" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="1163" height="226" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%201163%20226%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_new_oep" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_20  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 10: OEP Shellcode/PE Trickery</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_21  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>After the previous trickery in the new memory space, it will start creating another PE in memory, but this time the header does start with the MZ magic value. After building the headers, it will copy each PE section one at a time, as seen in <em>Figure 11</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_10">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="1511" height="724" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="1511" height="724" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%201511%20724%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_building_stage_2_pe" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_22  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 11: Building .text Section for Stage 2</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_23  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once the PE has been extracted to memory, it will make a direct call instead of using Threading APIs (same trickery as before). This can be seen in <em>Figure 12</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_11">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="652" height="96" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="652" height="96" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20652%2096%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2" title="BazarLoader-stage_1_call_stage_2" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_24  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 12: Calling Stage 2 Shellcode</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_25  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>BazarLoader’s stage 2 shellcode will make use of encrypted stack strings for many purposes<br />
throughout the rest of its code.</p>
<p>Before it continues with its malicious activity, it will check if the locale is Armenian (0x2b). Interestingly, instead of shutting down gracefully when the Armenian locale is detected, it will execute a <code class="language-markup">jmp</code> instruction to an invalid address, causing an access violation exception. We have seen Russian crimeware checking for the Armenian keyboard layout previously in malware such as KPot, we hypothesize this could be similar behavior.</p>
<p>To avoid running more than one instance of itself, BazarLoader will create a mutex with a hard-coded UUID, then use <code class="language-markup">kernel32.GetLastError</code> to check for the error <code class="language-markup">ERROR_ALREADY_EXISTS</code>. If the mutex already exists, it will exit the process. The call to <code class="language-markup">kernel32.CreateMutexA</code> can be seen in <em>Figure 13</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_12">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="556" height="479" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="556" height="479" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20556%20479%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_createmutex_0" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_26  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 13: Mutex Creation</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_27  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Interestingly, BazarLoader will check for mutexes twice.</p>
<p>Once completed, it will decyrpt its C2 configuration, as seen in <em>Figure 14</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_13">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="584" height="84" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="584" height="84" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20584%2084%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_decrypted_config" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_28  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 14: BazarLoader Stage 2 Decrypted Downloader Config</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_29  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner">Once BazarLoader has determined the Armenian language is not being used and another instance of itself is not running, it will make a HTTP HEAD request to <span style="color:#da291c;">hxxps://titlecs[.]com</span>. It will continue to do this until it receives a <code class="language-markup">200</code> response from the C2 server. The first request will be sent using <code class="language-markup">wininet.HttpSendRequestA</code>, as seen in <em>Figure 15</em>.</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_14">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="1331" height="499" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="1331" height="499" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%201331%20499%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request.png" alt="BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request" title="BazarLoader-stage_2_head_request" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_30  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 15: HTTP HEAD Request</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_31  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner">It is important to note that the HTTP header <code class="language-markup">Update</code>  is not a standard header and can be considered anomalous.</p>
<p>This HEAD request can be seen in <em>Figure 1</em>6.</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_15">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure16.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="690" height="111" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure16.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure16" title="BazarLoader-Figure16" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="690" height="111" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20690%20111%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure16.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure16" title="BazarLoader-Figure16" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_32  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 16: BazarLoader C2 Download Domain HEAD Request</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_33  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The C2 server will respond with a <code class="language-markup">200 OK</code> message.</p>
<p>BazarLoader will also check if it is connected to the internet by making a request to <em>microsoft[.]com</em>, as seen in <em>Figure 17</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_16">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure17.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="692" height="154" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure17.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure17" title="BazarLoader-Figure17" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="692" height="154" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20692%20154%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure17.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure17" title="BazarLoader-Figure17" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_34  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 17: BazarLoader Internet Connectivity Check</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_35  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once completed, it will make a POST request to the second domain in its configuration, as seen in <em>Figure 18</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_17">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure18.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="690" height="172" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure18.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure18" title="BazarLoader-Figure18" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="690" height="172" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20690%20172%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure18.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure18" title="BazarLoader-Figure18" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_36  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 18: BazarLoader C2 Checkin</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_37  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once completed, it will make a HTTP GET request in order to obtain the next stage, as seen in <em>Figure 19</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_18">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure19.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="691" height="649" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure19.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure19" title="BazarLoader-Figure19" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="691" height="649" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20691%20649%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-Figure19.png" alt="BazarLoader-Figure19" title="BazarLoader-Figure19" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_38  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 19: BazarLoader Downloading Encrypted Payload</em></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_2 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_2">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_2  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_39  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Differences Between Versions</h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_40  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>There are a few notable differences between the first version of BazarLoader sent on 2020-10-06 (Employment Termination Malspam) and the one sent on 2020-10-08 (Survey Malspam). The main difference between the two versions is the malware author(s) now include the string Stupid Defender to mock researchers, the shellcode that was stored in the <code class="language-markup">.data</code> section is now stored in the <code class="language-markup">.rsc</code> section, the functionality to get a pointer to the encrypted shellcode and to decrypt it have been broken out into their own separate functions. This can be seen in <em>Figures 20</em> and <em>21</em>.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_19">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode.png" target="_blank"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><noscript><img width="665" height="512" src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode.png" alt="BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode" title="BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode" /></noscript><img class="lazyload" width="665" height="512" src='data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20665%20512%22%3E%3C/svg%3E' data-src="https://www.gosecure.ai/wp-content/uploads/BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode.png" alt="BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode" title="BazarLoader-updated_decrypt_shellcode" /></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_41  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 20: Updated Main Shellcode Decryption/Execution Routine</em></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_20">

			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_43  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><em>Figure 22: Encrypted Shellcode in Resource Section</em></div>
			</div>

			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_3 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_3 et_pb_row_empty">
				
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_3  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_44  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Summary</h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_45  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>BazarLoader is becoming increasingly popular amongst threat actors. We suspect the reason behind the malware developer(s) success is their use of techniques such as avoiding the use of threading APIs and faking PE injection, when in reality, it is simply shellcode injection. These techniques are likely used to confuse Endpoint Detection and Response (EDR) solutions.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>[/et_<br />
pb_row]

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
  /*
   * Light YouTube Embeds by @labnol
   * Credit: https://www.labnol.org/
   */

  function labnolIframe(div) {
    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.setAttribute('src', 'https://www.youtube.com/embed/' + div.dataset.id + '?autoplay=1');
    iframe.setAttribute('frameborder', '0');
    iframe.setAttribute('allowfullscreen', '1');
    iframe.setAttribute('allow', 'accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture');
    div.parentNode.replaceChild(iframe, div);
  }

  function initYouTubeVideos() {
    var playerElements = document.querySelectorAll('.youtube-player');
    for (var n = 0; n < playerElements.length; n++) {
      var videoId = playerElements[n].dataset.id;
      var div = document.createElement('div');
      div.setAttribute('data-id', videoId);
      var thumbNode = document.createElement('img');
      thumbNode.src = '//i.ytimg.com/vi/ID/hqdefault.jpg'.replace('ID', videoId);
      div.appendChild(thumbNode);
      var playButton = document.createElement('div');
      playButton.setAttribute('class', 'play');
      div.appendChild(playButton);
      div.onclick = function () {
        labnolIframe(this);
      };
      playerElements[n].appendChild(div);
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initYouTubeVideos);
